Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 51, the initial release (though not the final mission release) of the Apollo 11 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software. The flown, final release was Comanche 55. The reconstruction is believed to be exactly accurate, but in the absence of an actual Apollo-era listing of Comanche 51, some explanation of the reconstruction process is needed to insure confidence in that accuracy.

The starting point was the source code of Comanche 55, whose original source code is available. Comanche 55 source code was then modified by undoing changes known to have been made between revisions 51 and 55. The most-significant steps involved reverting changes related to the R-2 lunar potential model, the details of which were known from the previous, separate, independent reconstruction of the Apollo 10 Lunar Module software Luminary 69/2. The now-reconstructed Comanche 51 source code was verified by assembling it and checking that the assembled code had the expected known-correct memory-bank checksums. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Comanche 55 or Luminary 69 printouts, although the source code would likely have different page numbers in a contemporary Comanche 51 listing.

Annotations that were not present in the contemporary source code have been added to the reconstructed code to justify each change relative to Comanche 55. Here's a guide to some of the Apollo documentation relevant to those annotations:
  • MIT/IL engineering drawing 2021153D, sheet 3. Listing of the memory-bank checksums for Comanche 51.
  • Comanche 55 (Apollo 11 CM final release) assembly listing.
  • Reconstructed Luminary69/2 (Apollo 10 LM final release) assembly listing.
  • Luminary 69 (Apollo 10 LM initial release) assembly listing.
  • Colossus 249 (Apollo 9 CM final release) assembly listing.
  • Programmed Guidance Equations for Colossus 2, Based on Comanche 55. A pseudocode representation of Comanche 55, showing change bars for differences from Comanche 45/2.
There is also a short writeup about the reconstruction process in our software repository that may be helpful.

Comments expected to have been present in the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC Project's GitHub repository. 

001557,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001558,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001559,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 051.
001560,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the
001561,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Command
001562,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 11.
001563,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Comanche 055. It
001564,000009:                                                                                                  ##              has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
001565,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Comanche 51 in NASA drawing
001566,000011:                                                                                                  ##              2021153D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
001567,000012:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
001568,000013:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 37-130
001569,000014:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001570,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001571,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001572,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-07-30 MAS  Created from Comanche 55. Removed new pad-
001573,000018:                                                                                                  ##                              loaded erasables for the R-2 potential model.
001574,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2020-12-12 RSB  Expanded the justifying annotations for the steps
001575,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              of Mike's reconstruction and made them consistent
001576,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              in style to similar annotations in Comanche 44.

Page 37 

001579,000024:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001580,000025: 
001581,000026:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001582,000027:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001583,000028:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001584,000029: 
001585,000030:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001586,000031:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001587,000032:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001588,000033: 
001589,000034:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001590,000035:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001591,000036:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001592,000037: 
001593,000038:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001594,000039:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001595,000040: 
001596,000041:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001597,000042: 
001598,000043:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001599,000044:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001600,000045: 
001601,000046:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001602,000047: 
001603,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001604,000049:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001605,000050: 
001606,000051:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001607,000052:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001608,000053:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001609,000054:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001610,000055:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001611,000056:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001612,000057: 
001613,000058:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001614,000059: 
001615,000060:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001616,000061:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001617,000062:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001618,000063:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001619,000064:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001620,000065:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001621,000066:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001622,000067:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001623,000068:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001624,000069:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001625,000070:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 38 

001627,000072:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001628,000073:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001629,000074:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001630,000075:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001631,000076:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001632,000077:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001633,000078:

001636,000081:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001637,000082: 
001638,000083: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001639,000084: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001640,000085: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001641,000086: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001642,000087: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001643,000088: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001644,000089: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001645,000090:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001646,000091: 
001647,000092: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001648,000093: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001649,000094: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001650,000095: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001651,000096: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001652,000097: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001653,000098: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001654,000099: 
001655,000100: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20

003045,001490:                                                                                                  #  (INTB15+ THROUGH RUPTMXM)             (32D)

003047,001492:    0115     0114               DSEXIT             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR DSPIN

003053,001498:    0116     0115               WDRET              EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR DSPWD
003054,001499:    0116     0115               DECRET             EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)

003056,001501: 
003057,001502:                                                                                                  #  THE REGISTERS BETWEEN ADDRWD AND PRIORITY MUST STAY IN THE FOLLOWING ORDER FOR INTERPRETIVE TRACE.
